

```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
import random
import requests as req
from citipy import citipy
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
import json
import csv
```


```python
#create a random list of lattitudes and longitudes
random_lat = []
for i in range (0,600):
    random_lat.append(random.randrange(-90,90))
random_lon = []
for i in range(0,600):
    random_lon.append(random.randrange(-180,180))
```


```python
#convert lists to dataframe and join them together, rename columns
random_lat = pd.DataFrame(data=random_lat).astype(float)
random_lon = pd.DataFrame(data=random_lon).astype(float)
random_coord = pd.concat([random_lat, random_lon], axis=1)
random_coord.columns = (['Lattitude', 'Longitude'])
```


```python
#create City Name column
random_coord['City Name'] = ""
#use citipy to convert coordinates to citipy object of nearest city via iterrows
for index, row in random_coord.iterrows():
    random_coord.at[index, 'City Name'] = citipy.nearest_city(row['Lattitude'], row['Longitude'])
#use citipy to convert citipy object into the city name via iterrows
for index, row in random_coord.iterrows():
    random_coord.at[index, 'City Name'] = row['City Name'].city_name
```

```python
#construct the query url
api_key = 'f732afc0f1e5dbe75f47d1704a104faa'
url = 'http://api.openweathermap.org/data/2.5/weather?'
units = 'imperial'
query_url = url + 'appid=' + api_key + '&units=' + units + '&q='
```


```python
#create an empty list to store the json file
weather_data = []
#loop through the list of random city names to build json results
for index, row in random_coord.iterrows():
    response = req.get(query_url + row['City Name']).json()
    #check for cod = 404 city not found error and skip
    if response['cod'] != '404':
        weather_data.append(response)
        print(query_url + " " + row['City Name'])
```

```python
#create lists of all data needed to graph using list comprehension
temp_data = [data.get('main').get('temp') for data in weather_data]
lattitude = [data.get('coord').get('lat') for data in weather_data]
humidity = [data.get('main').get('humidity') for data in weather_data]
cloudiness = [data.get('clouds').get('all') for data in weather_data]
wind_speed = [data.get('wind').get('speed') for data in weather_data]
city_name = [data.get('name') for data in weather_data]
```


```python
#roll up all lists into a dataframe
weather_df = pd.DataFrame({'Temp': temp_data,
                           'Lattitude': lattitude,
                           'Humidity': humidity,
                           'Cloudiness': cloudiness,
                           'Wind Speed': wind_speed,
                           'City Name': city_name})
weather_df.head()
```

```python
#create a scatterplot of lattitude as x value and temp as y value, save a png and show graph
sns.regplot(x=weather_df['Lattitude'], y=weather_df['Temp'], color = 'b', fit_reg=False)
sns.set(style='darkgrid')
plt.title('Temp vs Lattitude 2/28/18')
plt.savefig('Temp_vs_Lattitude.png')
plt.show()
```


![png](output_9_0.png)



```python
#create a scatterplot of lattitude as x value and humidity as y value, save a png and show graph
sns.regplot(x=weather_df['Lattitude'], y=weather_df['Humidity'], color = 'b', fit_reg=False)
sns.set(style='darkgrid')
plt.title('Humidity vs Lattitude 2/28/18')
plt.savefig('Humidity_vs_Lattitude.png')
plt.show()
```


![png](output_10_0.png)



```python
#create a scatterplot of lattitude as x value and cloudiness as y value, save a png and show graph
sns.regplot(x=weather_df['Lattitude'], y=weather_df['Cloudiness'], color = 'b', fit_reg=False)
sns.set(style='darkgrid')
plt.title('Cloudiness vs Lattitude 2/28/18')
plt.savefig('Cloudiness_vs_Lattitude.png')
plt.show()
```


![png](output_11_0.png)



```python
#create a scatterplot of lattitude as x value and wind speed as y value, save a png and show graph
sns.regplot(x=weather_df['Lattitude'], y=weather_df['Wind Speed'], color = 'b', fit_reg=False)
sns.set(style='darkgrid')
plt.title('Wind Speed vs Lattitude 2/28/18')
plt.savefig('Wind_Speed_vs_Lattitude.png')
plt.show()
```


![png](output_12_0.png)



```python
#The first written observation that I noticed is that the temp data vs lattitude
#shows that it is colder in the northern hemisphere right now.  This is to be
#expected as the winter months are in full effect.

#The second observation is there are more cities overall in the northern hemisphere
#compared to the southern.  I suspect there is just more landmass on the northern 
#side, leading to more cities.

#The third observation is that it is windier the further from the equator that you
#go.  It is almost the reverse of the temp graph, although the temp graph
#is much more defined in its clustering.  You also cannot have negative wind
#speed, making them look less alike as well.
```
